        <a name="2888708">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="2888708" data-highest-scored="1" data-parentid="2888508" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="347" id="answer-2888708" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="2888708">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="347" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             347
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/2888708/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             First, the default is not Arial. The default is Droid Sans.
            </p>
            <p>
             Second, to change to a different built-in font, use
             <code>
              android:typeface
             </code>
             in layout XML or
             <code>
              setTypeface()
             </code>
             in Java.
            </p>
            <p>
             Third, there is no Helvetica font in Android. The built-in choices are Droid Sans (
             <code>
              sans
             </code>
             ), Droid Sans Mono (
             <code>
              monospace
             </code>
             ), and Droid Serif (
             <code>
              serif
             </code>
             ). While you can bundle your own fonts with your application and use them via
             <code>
              setTypeface()
             </code>
             , bear in mind that font files are big and, in some cases, require licensing agreements (e.g.,
             <a href="http://www.linotype.com/526/helvetica-family.html" rel="noreferrer">
              Helvetica, a Linotype font
             </a>
             ).
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              EDIT
             </strong>
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              The Android design language relies on traditional typographic tools
  such as scale, space, rhythm, and alignment with an underlying grid.
  Successful deployment of these tools is essential to help users
  quickly understand a screen of information. To support such use of
  typography, Ice Cream Sandwich introduced a new type family named
  Roboto, created specifically for the requirements of UI and
  high-resolution screens.
             </p>
             <p>
              The current TextView framework offers Roboto in thin, light, regular
  and bold weights, along with an italic style for each weight. The
  framework also offers the Roboto Condensed variant in regular and bold
  weights, along with an italic style for each weight.
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             After ICS, android includes Roboto fonts style,
Read more
             <a href="http://developer.android.com/design/style/typography.html" rel="noreferrer">
              Roboto
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              EDIT 2
             </strong>
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              With the advent of Support Library 26, Android now supports custom fonts by 
  default. You can insert new fonts in
              <strong>
               res/fonts
              </strong>
              which can be set to TextViews individually either in XML or programmatically. The default font for the whole application can also be changed by defining it styles.xml The android developer documentation has a clear guide on this
              <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/ui/look-and-feel/fonts-in-xml.html" rel="noreferrer">
               here
              </a>
             </p>
            </blockquote>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="9820211">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>

             256
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

              </path>
             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>

             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/9820211/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             First download the
             <code>
              .ttf
             </code>
             file of the font you need (
             <code>
              arial.ttf
             </code>
             ). Place it in the
             <code>
              assets
             </code>
             folder. (Inside assets folder create new folder named
             <strong>
              fonts
             </strong>
             and place it inside it.) Use the following code to apply the font to your
             <code>
              TextView
             </code>
             :
            </p>
            <pre><code>Typeface type = Typeface.createFromAsset(getAssets(),"fonts/arial.ttf"); 
textView.setTypeface(type);
</code></pre>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="14551476">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/14551476/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You might want to create
             <strong>
              static class
             </strong>
             which will contain all the fonts. That way, you won't create the font multiple times which might impact badly on
             <strong>
              performance
             </strong>
             .
Just make sure that you create a
             <strong>
              sub-folder
             </strong>
             called "
             <strong>
              fonts
             </strong>
             " under "
             <strong>
              assets
             </strong>
             " folder.
            </p>
            <p>
             Do something like:
            </p>
            <pre><code>public class CustomFontsLoader {

public static final int FONT_NAME_1 =   0;
public static final int FONT_NAME_2 =   1;
public static final int FONT_NAME_3 =   2;

private static final int NUM_OF_CUSTOM_FONTS = 3;

private static boolean fontsLoaded = false;

private static Typeface[] fonts = new Typeface[3];

private static String[] fontPath = {
    "fonts/FONT_NAME_1.ttf",
    "fonts/FONT_NAME_2.ttf",
    "fonts/FONT_NAME_3.ttf"
};


/**
 * Returns a loaded custom font based on it's identifier. 
 * 
 * @param context - the current context
 * @param fontIdentifier = the identifier of the requested font
 * 
 * @return Typeface object of the requested font.
 */
public static Typeface getTypeface(Context context, int fontIdentifier) {
    if (!fontsLoaded) {
        loadFonts(context);
    }
    return fonts[fontIdentifier];
}


private static void loadFonts(Context context) {
    for (int i = 0; i &lt; NUM_OF_CUSTOM_FONTS; i++) {
        fonts[i] = Typeface.createFromAsset(context.getAssets(), fontPath[i]);
    }
    fontsLoaded = true;

}
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This way, you can get the font from everywhere in your application.
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="16166184" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="2888508" data-position-on-page="5" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="21" id="answer-16166184" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="16166184">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="21" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             21
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/16166184/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h3>
             Best practice ever
            </h3>
            <p>
             <strong>
              TextViewPlus.java:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>public class TextViewPlus extends TextView {
    private static final String TAG = "TextView";

    public TextViewPlus(Context context) {
        super(context);
    }

    public TextViewPlus(Context context, AttributeSet attrs) {
        super(context, attrs);
        setCustomFont(context, attrs);
    }

    public TextViewPlus(Context context, AttributeSet attrs, int defStyle) {
        super(context, attrs, defStyle);
        setCustomFont(context, attrs);
    }

    private void setCustomFont(Context ctx, AttributeSet attrs) {
        TypedArray a = ctx.obtainStyledAttributes(attrs, R.styleable.TextViewPlus);
        String customFont = a.getString(R.styleable.TextViewPlus_customFont);
        setCustomFont(ctx, customFont);
        a.recycle();
    }

    public boolean setCustomFont(Context ctx, String asset) {
        Typeface typeface = null;
        try {
            typeface = Typeface.createFromAsset(ctx.getAssets(), asset);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            Log.e(TAG, "Unable to load typeface: "+e.getMessage());
            return false;
        }

        setTypeface(typeface);
        return true;
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              attrs.xml:
             </strong>
             (Where to place
             <strong>
              res/values
             </strong>
             )
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?&gt;
&lt;resources&gt;
    &lt;declare-styleable name="TextViewPlus"&gt;
        &lt;attr name="customFont" format="string"/&gt;
    &lt;/declare-styleable&gt;
&lt;/resources&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              How to use:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?&gt;
&lt;LinearLayout 
    xmlns:android="http://schemas.android.com/apk/res/android"
    xmlns:foo="http://schemas.android.com/apk/res-auto"
    android:orientation="vertical" android:layout_width="fill_parent"
    android:layout_height="fill_parent"&gt;

    &lt;com.mypackage.TextViewPlus
        android:id="@+id/textViewPlus1"
        android:layout_height="match_parent"
        android:layout_width="match_parent"
        android:text="@string/showingOffTheNewTypeface"
        foo:customFont="my_font_name_regular.otf"&gt;
    &lt;/com.mypackage.TextViewPlus&gt;
&lt;/LinearLayout&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Hope this will help you.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="16166184">

        <a name="26226095">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="26226095" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="2888508" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="15" id="answer-26226095" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="26226095">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="15" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             15
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/26226095/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Another way to consolidate font creation...
            </p>
            <pre><code>public class Font {
  public static final Font  PROXIMA_NOVA    = new Font("ProximaNovaRegular.otf");
  public static final Font  FRANKLIN_GOTHIC = new Font("FranklinGothicURWBoo.ttf");
  private final String      assetName;
  private volatile Typeface typeface;

  private Font(String assetName) {
    this.assetName = assetName;
  }

  public void apply(Context context, TextView textView) {
    if (typeface == null) {
      synchronized (this) {
        if (typeface == null) {
          typeface = Typeface.createFromAsset(context.getAssets(), assetName);
        }
      }
    }
    textView.setTypeface(typeface);
  }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             And then to use in your activity...
            </p>
            <pre><code>myTextView = (TextView) findViewById(R.id.myTextView);
Font.PROXIMA_NOVA.apply(this, myTextView);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Mind you, this double-checked locking idiom with the volatile field only works correctly with the memory model used in Java 1.5+.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="44139820" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="2888508" data-position-on-page="8" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="13" id="answer-44139820" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="44139820">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             13
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

               </path>

             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/44139820/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h2>
             <strong>
              Best practice is to use Android Support Library version 26.0.0 or above.
             </strong>
            </h2>
            <p>
             <strong>
              STEP 1: add font file
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              In
              <em>
               res
              </em>
              folder create new
              <em>
               font
              </em>
              resource dictionary
             </li>
             <li>
              Add font file (
              <em>
               .ttf
              </em>
              ,
              <em>
               .orf
              </em>
              )
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             For example, when font file will be helvetica_neue.ttf that will generates R.font.helvetica_neue
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              STEP 2: create font family
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              In
              <em>
               font
              </em>
              folder add new resource file
             </li>
             <li>
              Enclose each font file, style, and weight attribute in the  element.
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             For example:
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?&gt;
&lt;font-family xmlns:android="http://schemas.android.com/apk/res/android"&gt;
    &lt;font
        android:fontStyle="normal"
        android:fontWeight="400"
        android:font="@font/helvetica_neue" /&gt;
&lt;/font-family&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              STEP 3: use it
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             In xml layouts:
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;TextView
    android:layout_width="wrap_content"
    android:layout_height="wrap_content"
    android:fontFamily="@font/my_font"/&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Or add fonts to style:
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;style name="customfontstyle" parent="@android:style/TextAppearance.Small"&gt;
    &lt;item name="android:fontFamily"&gt;@font/lobster&lt;/item&gt;
&lt;/style&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             For more examples you can follow documentation:
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              <a href="https://developer.android.com/preview/features/working-with-fonts.html" rel="noreferrer">
               Working with fonts
              </a>
             </p>
            </blockquote>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <a name="48763792">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="48763792" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="2888508" data-position-on-page="9" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="9" id="answer-48763792" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="48763792">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="9" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             9
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/48763792/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             When your font is stored inside
             <code>
              res/asset/fonts/Helvetica.ttf
             </code>
             use the following:
            </p>
            <pre><code>Typeface tf = Typeface.createFromAsset(getAssets(),"fonts/Helvetica.ttf"); 
txt.setTypeface(tf);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Or, if your font file is stores inside
             <code>
              res/font/helvetica.ttf
             </code>
             use the following:
            </p>
            <pre><code>Typeface tf = ResourcesCompat.getFont(this,R.font.helvetica);
txt.setTypeface(tf);
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="20225486" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="2888508" data-position-on-page="10" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="7" id="answer-20225486" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="20225486">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             It's a little old, but I improved the class CustomFontLoader a little bit and I wanted to share it so it can be helpfull. Just create a new class with this code.
            </p>
            <pre><code> import android.content.Context;
 import android.graphics.Typeface;

public enum FontLoader {

ARIAL("arial"),
TIMES("times"),
VERDANA("verdana"),
TREBUCHET("trbuchet"),
GEORGIA("georgia"),
GENEVA("geneva"),
SANS("sans"),
COURIER("courier"),
TAHOMA("tahoma"),
LUCIDA("lucida");   


private final String name;
private Typeface typeFace;


private FontLoader(final String name) {
    this.name = name;

    typeFace=null;  
}

public static Typeface getTypeFace(Context context,String name){
    try {
        FontLoader item=FontLoader.valueOf(name.toUpperCase(Locale.getDefault()));
        if(item.typeFace==null){                
            item.typeFace=Typeface.createFromAsset(context.getAssets(), "fonts/"+item.name+".ttf");                 
        }           
        return item.typeFace;
    } catch (Exception e) {         
        return null;
    }                   
}
public static Typeface getTypeFace(Context context,int id){
    FontLoader myArray[]= FontLoader.values();
    if(!(id&lt;myArray.length)){           
        return null;
    } 
    try {
        if(myArray[id].typeFace==null){     
            myArray[id].typeFace=Typeface.createFromAsset(context.getAssets(), "fonts/"+myArray[id].name+".ttf");                       
        }       
        return myArray[id].typeFace;    
    }catch (Exception e) {          
        return null;
    }   

}

public static Typeface getTypeFaceByName(Context context,String name){      
    for(FontLoader item: FontLoader.values()){              
        if(name.equalsIgnoreCase(item.name)){
            if(item.typeFace==null){
                try{
                    item.typeFace=Typeface.createFromAsset(context.getAssets(), "fonts/"+item.name+".ttf");     
                }catch (Exception e) {          
                    return null;
                }   
            }
            return item.typeFace;
        }               
    }
    return null;
}   

public static void loadAllFonts(Context context){       
    for(FontLoader item: FontLoader.values()){              
        if(item.typeFace==null){
            try{
                item.typeFace=Typeface.createFromAsset(context.getAssets(), "fonts/"+item.name+".ttf");     
            }catch (Exception e) {
                item.typeFace=null;
            }   
        }                
    }       
}   
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Then just use this code on you textview:
            </p>
            <pre><code> Typeface typeFace=FontLoader.getTypeFace(context,"arial");  
 if(typeFace!=null) myTextView.setTypeface(typeFace);
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="48851133" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="2888508" data-position-on-page="11" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="6" id="answer-48851133" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="48851133">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>

             6
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/48851133/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I finally got a very easy solution to this.
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               use these Support libraries in
               <strong>
                app level gradle
               </strong>
               ,
              </p>
              <pre><code>compile 'com.android.support:appcompat-v7:26.0.2'
compile 'com.android.support:support-v4:26.0.2'
</code></pre>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               then create a directory named
               <strong>
                "font"
               </strong>
               inside the
               <strong>
                res
               </strong>
               folder
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              put fonts(ttf) files in that font directory, keep in mind the naming conventions [e.g.name should not contain any special character, any uppercase character and any space or tab]
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               After that, reference that font from
               <strong>
                xml
               </strong>
               like this
              </p>
              <pre><code>        &lt;Button
        android:id="@+id/btn_choose_employee"
        android:layout_width="140dp"
        android:layout_height="40dp"
        android:layout_centerInParent="true"
        android:background="@drawable/rounded_red_btn"
        android:onClick="btnEmployeeClickedAction"
        android:text="@string/searching_jobs"
        android:textAllCaps="false"
        android:textColor="@color/white"
        android:fontFamily="@font/times_new_roman_test"
        /&gt;
</code></pre>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             In this example,
             <strong>
              <em>
               times_new_roman_test
              </em>
             </strong>
             is a font ttf file from that font directory
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="18482136">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/18482136/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <pre><code>import java.lang.ref.WeakReference;
import java.util.HashMap;

import android.content.Context;
import android.graphics.Typeface;

public class FontsManager {

    private static FontsManager instance;

    private static HashMap&lt;String, WeakReference&lt;Typeface&gt;&gt; typefaces = new HashMap&lt;String, WeakReference&lt;Typeface&gt;&gt;();

    private static Context context;

    private FontsManager(final Context ctx) {
        if (context == null) {
            context = ctx;
        }
    }

    public static FontsManager getInstance(final Context appContext) {
        if (instance == null) {
            instance = new FontsManager(appContext);
        }
        return instance;
    }

    public static FontsManager getInstance() {
        if (instance == null) {
            throw new RuntimeException(
                    "Call getInstance(Context context) at least once to init the singleton properly");
        }
        return instance;
    }

    public Typeface getFont(final String assetName) {
        final WeakReference&lt;Typeface&gt; tfReference = typefaces.get(assetName);
        if (tfReference == null || tfReference.get() == null) {
            final Typeface tf = Typeface.createFromAsset(context.getResources().getAssets(),
                    assetName);
            typefaces.put(assetName, new WeakReference&lt;Typeface&gt;(tf));
            return tf;
        }
        return tfReference.get();
    }

}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This way, you can create a View which inherits from TextView and calls setTypeface on its constructor.
            </p>
           </div>

           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             get font from  asset and set to all children
            </p>
            <pre><code>public static void overrideFonts(final Context context, final View v) {
    try {
        if (v instanceof ViewGroup) {
            ViewGroup vg = (ViewGroup) v;
            for (int i = 0; i &lt; vg.getChildCount(); i++) {
                View child = vg.getChildAt(i);
                overrideFonts(context, child);
         }
        } else if (v instanceof TextView ) {
            ((TextView) v).setTypeface(Typeface.createFromAsset(context.getAssets(),"DroidNaskh.ttf"));// "BKOODB.TTF"));
        }
    } catch (Exception e) {
 }
 } 
</code></pre>

           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <ol>
             <li>
              add class FontTextView.java:
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <br/>
            </p>
            <pre><code>public class FontTextView extends TextView {
    String fonts[] = {"HelveticaNeue.ttf", "HelveticaNeueLight.ttf", "motschcc.ttf", "symbol.ttf"};

    public FontTextView(Context context, AttributeSet attrs, int defStyle) {
        super(context, attrs, defStyle);
        init(attrs);
    }

    public FontTextView(Context context, AttributeSet attrs) {
        super(context, attrs);
        if (!isInEditMode()) {
            init(attrs);
        }

    }

    public FontTextView(Context context) {
        super(context);
        if (!isInEditMode()) {
            init(null);
        }
    }

    private void init(AttributeSet attrs) {
        if (attrs != null) {
            TypedArray a = getContext().obtainStyledAttributes(attrs, R.styleable.FontTextView);
            if (a.getString(R.styleable.FontTextView_font_type) != null) {
                String fontName = fonts[Integer.valueOf(a.getString(R.styleable.FontTextView_font_type))];

                if (fontName != null) {
                    Typeface myTypeface = Typeface.createFromAsset(getContext().getAssets(), "font/" + fontName);
                    setTypeface(myTypeface);
                }
                a.recycle();
            }
        }
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <br/>
            </p>
            <ol start="2">
             <li>
              add to assets library font
              <br/>
              <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/oiTuQ.png" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
               <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/oiTuQ.png"/>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <br/>
            </p>
            <ol start="3">
             <li>
              <p>
               add to attrs.xml ,
The numbers should be in the order in array class.
              </p>
              <pre><code>&lt;declare-styleable name="FontTextView"&gt;
&lt;attr name="font_type" format="enum"&gt;
    &lt;enum name="HelveticaNeue" value="0"/&gt;
    &lt;enum name="HelveticaNeueLight" value="1"/&gt;
    &lt;enum name="motschcc" value="2"/&gt;
    &lt;enum name="symbol" value="3"/&gt;
&lt;/attr&gt;
</code></pre>
              <p>
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <br/>
            </p>
            <ol start="4">
             <li>
              Select a font from the list
              <br/>
              <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/db8XU.png" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
               <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/db8XU.png"/>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="51144208" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="2888508" data-position-on-page="15" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1" id="answer-51144208" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="51144208">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/51144208/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Android uses the Roboto font, which is a really nice looking font, with several different weights (regular, light, thin, condensed) that look great on high density screens.
            </p>
            <p>
             Check below link to check roboto fonts:
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/34444616/how-to-use-roboto-in-xml-layout/34445295#34445295">
              How to use Roboto in xml layout
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Back to your question, if you want to change the font for
             <strong>
              all of the TextView/Button in your app
             </strong>
             , try adding below code into your styles.xml to use
             <strong>
              Roboto-light
             </strong>
             font:
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;!-- Base application theme. --&gt;
&lt;style name="AppTheme" parent="Theme.AppCompat.Light.DarkActionBar"&gt;
    &lt;!-- Customize your theme here. --&gt;
    ......
    &lt;item name="android:buttonStyle"&gt;@style/MyButton&lt;/item&gt;
    &lt;item name="android:textViewStyle"&gt;@style/MyTextView&lt;/item&gt;
&lt;/style&gt;

&lt;style name="MyButton" parent="@style/Widget.AppCompat.Button"&gt;
    &lt;item name="android:textAllCaps"&gt;false&lt;/item&gt;
    &lt;item name="android:fontFamily"&gt;sans-serif-light&lt;/item&gt;
&lt;/style&gt;

&lt;style name="MyTextView" parent="@style/TextAppearance.AppCompat"&gt;
    &lt;item name="android:fontFamily"&gt;sans-serif-light&lt;/item&gt;
&lt;/style&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             And don't forget to use 'AppTheme' in your AndroidManifest.xml
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;application
    android:allowBackup="true"
    android:icon="@mipmap/ic_launcher"
    android:label="@string/app_name"
    android:roundIcon="@mipmap/ic_launcher_round"
    android:supportsRtl="true"
    android:theme="@style/AppTheme"&gt;
    ......
&lt;/application&gt;
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <a name="38728710">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="38728710" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="2888508" data-position-on-page="16" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="0" id="answer-38728710" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="38728710">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="0" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             0
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/38728710/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Maybe something a bit simpler:
            </p>
            <pre><code>public class Fonts {
  public static HashSet&lt;String,Typeface&gt; fonts = new HashSet&lt;&gt;();

  public static Typeface get(Context context, String file) {
    if (! fonts.contains(file)) {
      synchronized (this) {
        Typeface typeface = Typeface.createFromAsset(context.getAssets(), name);
        fonts.put(name, typeface);
      }
    }
    return fonts.get(file);
  }
}

// Usage
Typeface myFont = Fonts.get("arial.ttf");
</code></pre>
            <p>
             (Note this code is untested, but in general this approach should work well.)
            </p>
           </div>
